alias -g jp='| '\''builtin'\'' command perl -lanE '\''say __________'\'
alias jpf=\''builtin'\'' command perl -e '\''print `__________`for(__________)'\'
alias jpg=\''builtin'\'' command perl -e '\''print `__________ "$_"`for<*>'\'
alias -g jr='|& '\''builtin'\'' command rg -v '\''\brg\b'\'' |& \rg --hidden --color=always -i --'

alias -g jt='| tr '\''__________'\'' '\''__________'\'

alias -g ju='| awk '\''{print $1}'\'' | uniq -c | sort -rn | head -10'
alias -g juu='| awk '\''{__________}'\'' | uniq -c | sort -rn | head -10'
alias -g jv='| pbcopy'
alias -g jwc='| wc -l'

alias -g jz=$'| fzf --ansi --prompt=\'<<)ZPWR(>> \' --bind=ctrl-n:page-down,ctrl-p:page-up,tab:toggle+down,ctrl-j:down,ctrl-k:up --preview \'test -z $file && file=$(echo {} | sed "s@^~@/Users/annieehler@");\nif test -f $file;then\n    if print -r -- $file | command egrep -iq "\\.[jw]ar$";then jar tf $file | bat --paging never --wrap character --color always --style="numbers,grid,changes,header" -l java --;\n    elif print -r -- $file | command egrep -iq "\\.(tgz|tar|tar\\.gz)$";then tar tf $file | bat --paging never --wrap character --color always --style="numbers,grid,changes,header" -l c --;\n    elif print -r -- $file | command egrep -iq "\\.deb$";then stat | bat --paging never --wrap character --color always --style="numbers,grid,changes,header"  -l sh --;\n    elif print -r -- $file | command egrep -iq "\\.rpm$";then stat | bat --paging never --wrap character --color always --style="numbers,grid,changes,header"  -l sh --;\n    elif print -r -- $file | command egrep -iq "\\.zip$";then unzip -v -- $file | bat --paging never --wrap character --color always --style="numbers,grid,changes,header" -l c --;\n    elif print -r -- $file | command egrep -iq "\\.(bzip|bz)$";then bzip -c -d $file | bat --paging never --wrap character --color always --style="numbers,grid,changes,header" -l yaml --;\n    elif print -r -- $file | command egrep -iq "\\.(bzip2|bz2)$";then bzip2 -c -d $file | bat --paging never --wrap character --color always --style="numbers,grid,changes,header" -l yaml --;\n    elif print -r -- $file | command egrep -iq "\\.(xzip|xz)$";then xz -c -d $file | bat --paging never --wrap character --color always --style="numbers,grid,changes,header" -l yaml --;\n    elif print -r -- $file | command egrep -iq "\\.(gzip|gz)$";then gzip -c -d $file | bat --paging never --wrap character --color always --style="numbers,grid,changes,header" -l yaml --;\n    elif print -r -- $file | command egrep -iq "\\.(so|dylib).*$";then\n        zsh /Users/annieehler/.zpwr/scripts/zpwrClearList.zsh -- $file | fold -s -w 80\n        nm $file | bat --paging never --wrap character --color always --style="numbers,grid,changes,header" -l yaml --\n        xxd $file | bat --paging never --wrap character --color always --style="numbers,grid,changes,header" -l yaml --\n    else\n        if LC_MESSAGES=C command grep -Hm1 -- "^" "$file" 2>&1 | command grep -iq "binary";then\n            zsh /Users/annieehler/.zpwr/scripts/zpwrClearList.zsh -- $file | fold -s -w 80\n            test -x $file && objdump -d $file | bat --paging never --wrap character --color always --style="numbers,grid,changes,header" -l yaml --\n            xxd $file | bat --paging never --wrap character --color always --style="numbers,grid,changes,header" -l yaml --\n        else\n                        base=${file##*/}\n            case $base in\n                (*.txt)\n                    bat --paging never --wrap character --color always --style="numbers,grid,changes,header" -l ASP -- "$file" 2>/dev/null;\n                    ;;\n                ([!.]*.*)\n                    bat --paging never --wrap character --color always --style="numbers,grid,changes,header" -- "$file" 2>/dev/null;\n                    ;;\n                (.*.*)\n                    bat --paging never --wrap character --color always --style="numbers,grid,changes,header" -- "$file" 2>/dev/null;\n                    ;;\n                (*)\n                    bat --paging never --wrap character --color always --style="numbers,grid,changes,header" -l ASP -- "$file" 2>/dev/null;\n                    ;;\n            esac\n        fi\n    fi\nelse\n    zsh /Users/annieehler/.zpwr/scripts/zpwrClearList.zsh -- $file | fold -s -w 80\nfi\' '
alias -g jza='"$($ZPWR_FZF --prompt='\''<<)ZPWR(>> '\'' --bind=ctrl-n:page-down,ctrl-p:page-up,tab:toggle+down,ctrl-j:down,ctrl-k:up --preview "[[ -f {} ]] && bat --paging never --wrap character --color always --style="numbers,grid,changes,header" -- {}__________  2>/dev/null | cat -n || stat -- {} | fold -80 | head -500")"'
